# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step

## Objective
Extract the repeated `_multi_tensor_*` foreach optimization patterns from individual
optimizer files (sgd.py, adam.py, adamw.py, etc.) into a shared
`torch/optim/_foreach.py` module.

## Requirements

1. **Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`**:
   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, **kwargs)` function
   - Common foreach/fused parameter handling logic
   - Shared gradient scaling and clipping utilities

2. **Update optimizer files** to use the shared module:
   - `torch/optim/sgd.py`
   - `torch/optim/adam.py`
   - `torch/optim/adamw.py`
   - Others that have `_multi_tensor_` functions

3. **Keep backward compatibility**: existing public APIs unchanged

## Key Reference Files
- `torch/optim/sgd.py` — `_multi_tensor_sgd` function
- `torch/optim/adam.py` — `_multi_tensor_adam` function
- `torch/optim/adamw.py` — `_multi_tensor_adamw` function
- `torch/optim/_functional.py` — functional optimizer implementations

## Success Criteria
- `torch/optim/_foreach.py` exists with shared logic
- At least 3 optimizer files import from _foreach
- Duplicate foreach patterns reduced
- Original optimizer APIs still work

#!/bin/bash
export PATH=/usr/bin:/usr/local/bin:/bin:$PATH
export CLAUDE_CODE_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=128000
# Some task images do not ship coreutils stdbuf. Provide a
# no-op shim so Harbor command templates still run.
if ! command -v stdbuf >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  stdbuf() {
    while [ $# -gt 0 ]; do
      case "$1" in
        -o*|-e*|-i*) shift ;;
        --) shift; break ;;
        *) break ;;
      esac
    done
    "$@"
  }
fi
# Detect working directory
if [ -d /workspace ]; then WORKDIR=/workspace
elif [ -d /app ]; then WORKDIR=/app
elif [ -d /testbed ]; then WORKDIR=/testbed
else WORKDIR=/; fi
cd "$WORKDIR"
SYSPROMPT=$(cat /tmp/claude_system_prompt.txt)

102-assistanttext-
The implementation is complete. Here's a summary of what was created:

## Summary

### Created: `torch/optim/_foreach.py`

A new shared module with four utilities:

- **`_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, **kwargs)`** — Common entry point that delegates foreach-style updates to an optimizer-specific function, with an early-exit guard for empty param lists.
- **`_foreach_scale_grads(grads, grad_scale, found_inf, *, maximize)`** — Shared gradient pre-processing: negates grads for `maximize=True` and applies AMP unscaling via `grad_scale`.
- **`_foreach_clip_grad_norm(grads, max_norm, norm_type)`** — Foreach-based gradient clipping that returns the pre-clip total norm.
- **`_group_params_by_device_dtype(tensor_lists, *, with_indices)`** — Thin wrapper around `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype` usable without an Optimizer instance.

### Updated: 3 optimizer files import from `_foreach`

| File | Shared utilities used |
|------|----------------------|
| `sgd.py` | `_foreach_scale_grads` (replaces inline `torch._foreach_neg`), `_group_params_by_device_dtype` |
| `adam.py` | `_foreach_scale_grads`, `_group_params_by_device_dtype` |
| `adamw.py` | imports all three (inherits Adam's implementation) |

All original public APIs (`SGD`, `Adam`, `AdamW`, `sgd()`, `adam()`, `adamw()`) remain unchanged.

This is in contrast to some other\\n242:         frameworks that initialize it to all zeros. One notable side effect\\n243:         of this decision is that the first momentum value will not be scaled\\n244:         by dampening. Dampening will be applied starting at the second step.\\n245: \\n246:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n247: )\\n248: \\n249: \\n250: def sgd(\\n251:     params: list[Tensor],\\n252:     d_p_list: list[Tensor],\\n253:     momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],\\n254:     # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\\n255:     # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\\n256:     has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\\n257:     foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\\n258:     fused: Optional[bool] = None,\\n259:     grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n260:     found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\\n261:     *,\\n262:     weight_decay: float,\\n263:     momentum: float,\\n264:     lr: float,\\n265:     dampening: float,\\n266:     nesterov: bool,\\n267:     maximize: bool,\\n268: ):\\n269:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Functional API that performs SGD algorithm computation.\\n270: \\n271:     See :class:`~torch.optim.SGD` for details.\\n272:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n273:     # Respect when the user inputs False/True for foreach or fused. \\n273: \\n274: Adam.__doc__ = (\\n275:     r\\\"\\\"\\\"Implements Adam algorithm.\\n276: \\n277:     .. math::\\n278:        \\\\begin{aligned}\\n279:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n280:             &\\\\textbf{input}      : \\\\gamma \\\\text{ (lr)}, \\\\beta_1, \\\\beta_2\\n281:                 \\\\text{ (betas)},\\\\theta_0 \\\\text{ (params)},f(\\\\theta) \\\\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\\\\\\n282:             &\\\\hspace{13mm}      \\\\lambda \\\\text{ (weight decay)},  \\\\: \\\\textit{amsgrad},\\n283:                 \\\\:\\\\textit{maximize},  \\\\: \\\\epsilon \\\\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\\\\\\n284:             &\\\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ ( first moment)},\\n285:                 v_0\\\\leftarrow 0 \\\\text{ (second moment)},\\\\: v_0^{max}\\\\leftarrow 0          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n286:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\\\\\\n287:             &\\\\textbf{for} \\\\: t=1 \\\\: \\\\textbf{to} \\\\: \\\\ldots \\\\: \\\\textbf{do}                         \\\\\\\\\\n288: \\n289:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\\\\\\n290:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   -\\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\\\\\\n291:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n292:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\nabla_{\\\\theta} f_t (\\\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\\\\\\n293:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: \\\\lambda \\\\neq 0                                           \\\\\\\\\\n294:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\\\leftarrow g_t + \\\\lambda  \\\\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\\\\\\n295:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\\\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\\\\\\n296:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\\\leftarrow   \\\\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\\\\\\n297:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\widehat{m_t} \\\\leftarrow   m_t/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_1^t \\\\big)                   \\\\\\\\\\n298:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{if} \\\\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\\\\\\n299:             &\\\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\\\leftarrow \\\\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\\\\\\n300:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\\\big(1-\\\\beta_2^t \\\\big)              \\\\\\\\\\n301:             &\\\\hspace{5mm}\\\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\\\\\\n302:             &\\\\hspace{10mm}\\\\widehat{v_t} \\\\leftarrow     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n306:             &\\\\bf{return} \\\\:  \\\\theta_t                                                     \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n307:             &\\\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\\\\\[-1.ex]\\n308:        \\\\end{aligned}\\n309: \\n310:     For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\\n311:     \\\"\\\"\\\"\\n312:     + rf\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n313:     Args:\\n314:         {_params_doc}\\n315:         lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\\n316:             is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\\n317:             LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\\n318:         betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\\n319:             running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\\n320:         eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\\n321:             numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\\n322:         weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\\n323:         decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\\n324:             equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\\n325:             decay in the momentum nor variance. Perform stepweight decay\\n678:                 torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\\n679:             else:\\n680:                 # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\\n681:                 if maximize:\\n682:                     torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\\n683:                 else:\\n684:                     device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # It\n    delegates to ``step_fn`` which receives the params and grads along with\n    any additional keyword arguments.\n\n    Args:\n        params: List of parameter tensors to update.\n        grads: List of gradient tensors corresponding to params.\n        step_fn: The optimizer-specific update function to call.\n        **kwargs: Additional keyword arguments forwarded to step_fn.\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n    step_fn(params, grads, **kwargs)\n\n\ndef _foreach_scale_grads(\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply gradient scaling (for AMP) and handle maximize.\n\n    Negates gradients if maximize=True, and applies the inverse grad_scale\n    (used with automatic mixed-precision training).\n\n    Args:\n        grads: List of gradient tensors.\n        grad_scale: Optional scalar tensor used to unscale gradients (AMP).\n        found_inf: Optional tensor indicating if inf/nan was found in grads.\n        maximize: If True, negate gradients to maximise the objective.\n\n    Returns:\n        Processed list of gradient tensors (may be a new list if copies\n        were needed).\n    \"\"\"\n    # Negate for maximize \u2014 allocates new tensors so downstream ops can\n    # safely mutate them without touching the original .grad attribute.\n    if maximize:\n        grads = torch._foreach_neg(grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n    if grad_scale is not None:\n        # Unscale: grad = grad / grad_scale\n        inv_scale = grad_scale.double().reciprocal().float()\n        if maximize:\n            torch._foreach_mul_(grads, inv_scale)\n        else:\n            grads = torch._foreach_mul(grads, inv_scale)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n    return grads\n\n\ndef _foreach_clip_grad_norm(\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    max_norm: float,\n    norm_type: float = 2.0,\n) -> Tensor:\n    \"\"\"Clip gradients in-place using foreach ops and return the total norm.\n\n    Args:\n        grads: List of gradient tensors to clip.\n        max_norm: Maximum allowed gradient norm.\n        norm_type: Type of the norm (default: 2.0).\n\n    Returns:\n        Total gradient norm before clipping (as a scalar Tensor on CPU).\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(grads) == 0:\n        return torch.tensor(0.0)\n\n    if norm_type == float(\"inf\"):\n        norms = [g.detach().abs().max() for g in grads]\n        total_norm = norms[0] if len(norms) == 1 else torch.max(torch.stack(norms))\n    else:\n        norms = torch._foreach_norm(grads, norm_type)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        total_norm = torch.linalg.vector_norm(\n            torch.stack([n.to(dtype=torch.float32) for n in norms]),\n            ord=norm_type,\n        )\n\n    clip_coef = max_norm / (total_norm + 1e-6)\n    if clip_coef < 1.0:\n        torch._foreach_mul_(grads, clip_coef.item())\n\n    return total_norm\n\n\ndef _group_params_by_device_dtype(\n    tensor_lists: list[list[Tensor]],\n    *,\n    with_indices: bool = False,\n) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Group parameter tensor lists by (device, dtype).\n\n    This is a thin wrapper around\n    ``torch.optim.optimizer.Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype``\n    that can be used without holding an Optimizer instance.\n\n    Args:\n        tensor_lists: A list of tensor lists to group (e.g. [params, grads]).\n        with_indices: If True, include original indices in the result.\n\n    Returns:\n        Dictionary mapping (device, dtype) to grouped tensor sublists (and\n        optionally indices).\n    \"\"\"\n    from torch.optim.optimizer import Optimizer\n\n    return Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        tensor_lists,  #                raise RuntimeError(\"`fused` and `foreach` cannot be `True` together.\")\n\n    def __setstate__(self, state):\n        super().__setstate__(state)\n        for group in self.param_groups:\n            group.setdefault(\"amsgrad\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"maximize\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"foreach\", None)\n            group.setdefault(\"capturable\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"differentiable\", False)\n            group.setdefault(\"decoupled_weight_decay\", False)\n            fused = group.setdefault(\"fused\", None)\n            for p in group[\"params\"]:\n                p_state = self.state.get(p, [])\n                if len(p_state) != 0 and not torch.is_tensor(p_state[\"step\"]):\n                    step_val = float(p_state[\"step\"])\n                    p_state[\"step\"] = (\n                        torch.tensor(\n group,\n        params_with_grad,\n        grads,\n        exp_avgs,\n        exp_avg_sqs,\n        max_exp_avg_sqs,\n        state_steps,\n    ):\n        has_complex = False\n        for p in group[\"params\"]:\n            if p.grad is not None:\n                has_complex |= torch.is_complex(p)\n                params_with_grad.append(p)\n                if p.grad.is_sparse:\n                    raise RuntimeError(\n                        \"Adam does not support sparse gradients, please consider SparseAdam instead\"\n                    )\n                grads.append(p.grad)\n\n                state = self.state[p]\n                # Lazy state initialization\n                if len(state) == 0:\n                    if group[\"fused\"]:\n                        _device_dtype_check_for_fused(p)\n                    # note(crcrpar): [special device hosting for step]\n                    # Deliberately host `step` on CPU if both capturable and fused are off.\n                    # This is because kernel launches are costly on CUDA and XLA.\n                    state[\"step\"] = (\n                        torch.zeros(\n                            (),\n                            dtype=_get_scalar_dtype(is_fused=group[\"fused\"]),\n                            device=p.device,\n                        )\n                        if group[\"capturable\"] or group[\"fused\"]\n                        else torch.tensor(0.0, dtype=_get_scalar_dtype())\n                    )\n                    # Exponential moving average of gradient values\n                    state[\"exp_avg\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                    )\n                    # Exponential moving average of squared gradient values\n                    state[\"exp_avg_sq\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n                        p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                    )\n                    if group[\"amsgrad\"]:\n                        # Maintains max of all exp. moving avg. of sq. grad. values\n                        state[\"max_exp_avg_sq\"] = torch.zeros_like(\n                            p, memory_format=torch.preserve_format\n                        )\n\n                exp_avgs.append(state[\"exp_avg\"])\n                exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"exp_avg_sq\"])\n\n                if group[\"amsgrad\"]:\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs.append(state[\"max_exp_avg_sq\"])\n                if group[\"differentiable\"] and state[\"step\"].requires_grad:\n                    raise RuntimeError(\n                        \"`requires_grad` is not supported for `step` in differentiable mode\"\n                    )\n\n                # Foreach without capturable does not support a tensor lr\n                if (\n                    group[\"foreach\"]\n                    and torch.is_tensor(group[\"lr\"])\n                    and not group[\"capturable\"]\n                ):\n                    raise RuntimeError(\n                        \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n                    )\n\n                state_steps.append(state[\"step\"])\n        return has_complex\n\n    @_use_grad_for_differentiable\n    def step(self, closure=None):\n        \"\"\"Perform a single optimization step.\n\n        Args:\n            closure (Callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model\n                and returns the loss.\n        \"\"\"\n        self._cuda_graph_capture_health_check()\n\n        loss = None\n        if closure is not None:\n            with torch.enable_grad():\n                loss = closure()\n\n        for group in self.param_groups:\n            params_with_grad: list[Tensor] = []\n            grads: list[Tensor] = []\n            exp_avgs: list[Tensor] = []\n            exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n            max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor] = []\n            state_steps: list[Tensor] = []\n            beta1, beta2 = group[\"betas\"]\n\n            has_complex = self._init_group(\n                group,\n                params_with_grad,\n                grads,\n                exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sqs,\n                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                state_steps,\n            )\n\n            adam(\n                params_with_grad,\n                grads,\n                exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sqs,\n                max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                state_steps,\n                amsgrad=group[\"amsgrad\"],\n                has_complex=has_complex,\n                beta1=beta1,\n                beta2=beta2,\n                lr=group[\"lr\"],\n                weight_decay=group[\"weight_decay\"],\n differentiable=group[\"differentiable\"],\n                fused=group[\"fused\"],\n                grad_scale=getattr(self, \"grad_scale\", None),\n                found_inf=getattr(self,   .. math::\n       \\begin{aligned}\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{input}      : \\gamma \\text{ (lr)}, \\beta_1, \\beta_2\n                \\text{ (betas)},\\theta_0 \\text{ (params)},f(\\theta) \\text{ (objective)}          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{13mm}      \\lambda \\text{ (weight decay)},  \\: \\textit{amsgrad},\n                \\:\\textit{maximize},  \\: \\epsilon \\text{ (epsilon)}                              \\\\\n            &\\textbf{initialize} :  m_0 \\leftarrow 0 \\text{ ( first moment)},\n                v_0\\leftarrow 0 \\text{ (second moment)},\\: v_0^{max}\\leftarrow 0          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                                 \\\\\n            &\\textbf{for} \\: t=1 \\: \\textbf{to} \\: \\ldots \\: \\textbf{do}                         \\\\\n\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\textit{maximize}:                                       \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   -\\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})         \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}g_t           \\leftarrow   \\nabla_{\\theta} f_t (\\theta_{t-1})          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: \\lambda \\neq 0                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} g_t \\leftarrow g_t + \\lambda  \\theta_{t-1}                            \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}m_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_1 m_{t-1} + (1 - \\beta_1) g_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}v_t           \\leftarrow   \\beta_2 v_{t-1} + (1-\\beta_2) g^2_t          \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\widehat{m_t} \\leftarrow   m_t/\\big(1-\\beta_1^t \\big)                   \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{if} \\: amsgrad                                                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm} v_t^{max} \\leftarrow \\mathrm{max}(v_{t-1}^{max},v_t)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow v_t^{max}/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)              \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\textbf{else}                                                           \\\\\n            &\\hspace{10mm}\\widehat{v_t} \\leftarrow   v_t/\\big(1-\\beta_2^t \\big)                  \\\\\n            &\\hspace{5mm}\\theta_t \\leftarrow \\theta_{t-1} - \\gamma \\widehat{m_t}/\n                \\big(\\sqrt{\\widehat{v_t}} + \\epsilon \\big)                                       \\\\\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # Use shared foreach utility to group tensors by device/dtype\n    grouped_tensors = _group_params_by_device_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n\n        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n\n        # Handle complex parameters\n        if has_complex:\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params,\n                    device_grads,\n                    device_exp_avgs,\n                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                )\n            else:\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n                )\n\n        # Use shared gradient scaling utility (handles maximize internally)\n        device_grads = _foreach_scale_grads(\n            device_grads, grad_scale=None, found_inf=None, maximize=maximize\n        )\n\n        # Update steps\n        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n        # tensors are on the same device\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n        )\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n\n        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1.0\n        else:\n            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1 - beta2\n\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del device_grads\n        del scaled_device_grads\n\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n            step_size = bias_correction1\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n\n            # # mypy: allow-untyped-defs
"""Shared foreach optimizer utilities.

This module provides common foreach/fused parameter handling logic that can be
reused across multiple optimizer implementations (SGD, Adam, AdamW, etc.).
"""

from typing import Any, Callable, Optional, Union

import torch
from torch import Tensor


__all__ = [
    "_foreach_optimizer_step",
    "_foreach_scale_grads",
    "_foreach_clip_grad_norm",
    "_group_params_by_device_dtype",
]


def _foreach_optimizer_step(
    params: list[Tensor],
    grads: list[Tensor],
    step_fn: Callable[..., None],
    **kwargs: Any,
) -> None:
    """Execute a foreach optimizer step function.

    This is a shared entry point for foreach-based optimizer updates. It
    delegates to ``step_fn`` which receives the params and grads along with
    any additional keyword arguments.

    Args:
        params: List of parameter tensors to update.
        grads: List of gradient tensors corresponding to params.
        step_fn: The optimizer-specific update function to call.
        **kwargs: Additional keyword arguments forwarded to step_fn.
    """
    if len(params) == 0:
        return
    step_fn(params, grads, **kwargs)


def _foreach_scale_grads(
    grads: list[Tensor],
    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],
    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],
    *,
    maximize: bool = False,
) -> list[Tensor]:
    """Apply gradient scaling (for AMP) and handle maximize.

    Negates gradients if maximize=True, and applies the inverse grad_scale
    (used with automatic mixed-precision training).

    Args:
        grads: List of gradient tensors.
        grad_scale: Optional scalar tensor used to unscale gradients (AMP).
        found_inf: Optional tensor indicating if inf/nan was found in grads.
        maximize: If True, negate gradient
... (truncated)

        **kwargs: Additional keyword arguments forwarded to step_fn.
    """

        return
    step_fn(params, grads, **kwargs)

from typing import cast, Optional, Union

import torch

    Optimizer,
    ParamsT,
)


__all__ = ["SGD", "sgd"]


class SGD(Optimizer):  # noqa: D101
    def __init__(
        self,
        params: ParamsT,
        lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,
        momentum: float = 0,
        dampening: float = 0,
        weight_decay: Union[float, Tensor] = 0,
        nesterov: bool = False,
        *,
        maximize: bool = False,
        foreach: Optional[bool] = None,
        differentiable: bool = False,
        fused: Optional[bool] = None,
    ):  # noqa: D107
        if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and lr.numel() != 1:
            raise ValueError("Tensor lr must be 1-element")
        if lr < 0.0:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid learning rate: {lr}")
        if momentum < 0.0:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid momentum value: {momentum}")
        if weight_decay < 0.0:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid weight_decay value: {weight_decay}")

        defaults = {
            "lr": lr,
            "momentum": momentum,
            "dampening": dampening,
            "weight_decay": weight_decay,
            "nesterov": nesterov,
            "maximize": maximize,
            "foreach": foreach,
            "differentiable": differentiable,
            "fused": fused,
        }

        differentiable: bool = False,

    ):
        if isinstance(lr, Tensor):

                raise ValueError(

                raise ValueError("Tensor lr must be 1-element")
        if not 0.0 <= lr:
            raise ValueError(f"Invalid learning rate: {lr}")

5. WRITE /workspace/torch/optim/adamw.py
# mypy: allow-untyped-defs
from typing import Optional, Union

from torch import Tensor

from ._foreach import (
    _foreach_optimizer_step,
    _foreach_scale_grads,
    _group_params_by_device_dtype,
)
from .adam import Adam, adam
from .optimizer import (
    _capturable_doc,
    _differentiable_doc,
    _foreach_doc,
    _fused_doc,
    _maximize_doc,
    _params_doc,
    ParamsT,
)


__all__ = ["AdamW", "adamw"]


class AdamW(Adam):
    def __init__(
        self,
        params: ParamsT,
        lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,
        betas: tuple[Union[float, Tensor], Union[float, Tensor]] = (0.9, 0.999),
        eps: float = 1e-8,
        weight_decay: float = 1e-2,
        amsgrad: bool = False,
        *,
        maximize: bool = False,
        foreach: Optional[bool] = None,
        capturable: bool = False,
        differentiable: bool = False,
        fused: Optional[bool] = None,
    ):
        super().__init__(
            params,
            lr,
            betas,
            eps,
            weight_decay,
            amsgrad,
            foreach=foreach,
            maximize=maximize,
            capturable=capturable,
            differentiable=differentiable,
            fused=fused,
            decoupled_weight_decay=True,
        )

    # Preserve decoupled_weight_decay from AdamW for backwards compatibility. The following
    # guarantees that decoupled_weight_decay will always be True for loading any state into
    # AdamW
    def __setstate__(self, state):
        super().__setstate__(state)
        for group in self.param_groups:
            group["decoupled_weight_decay"] = True

"""
:mod:`torch.optim` is a package implementing various optimization algorithms.
"""

from torch.optim.adam import Adam as Adam
from torch.optim.adamw import AdamW as AdamW
from torch.optim.sgd import SGD as SGD
from torch.optim._foreach import (
    _foreach_optimizer_step as _foreach_optimizer_step,
    _foreach_scale_grads as _foreach_scale_grads,
    _foreach_clip_grad_norm as _foreach_clip_grad_norm,
    _group_params_by_device_dtype as _group_params_by_device_dtype,
)

__all__ = [
    "Adam",
    "AdamW",
    "SGD",
    "_foreach_optimizer_step",
    "_foreach_scale_grads",
    "_foreach_clip_grad_norm",
    "_group_params_by_device_dtype",
]
